teamPlanEndDateTo: teamPlanEndDateTo ?? this.teamPlanEndDateTo,\n      extendToNextTeamPlan: extendToNextTeamPlan ?? this.extendToNextTeamPlan,\n      isDeletionScheduled: isDeletionScheduled ??
